Changelog

Date Author Change
2021-08-06 Jonathan Wakely <jwakely at redhat dot com> - 1.18-4 - Rebuilt for Boost 1.76
2021-07-21 Fedora Release Engineering <releng at fedoraproject dot org> - 1.18-3 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_35_Mass_Rebuild
2021-06-29 Jerry James <loganjerry at gmail dot com> - 1.18-2 - Rebuild for ntl 11.5.1
2021-06-17 Jerry James <loganjerry at gmail dot com> - 1.18-1 - Version 1.18
2021-02-18 Jerry James <loganjerry at gmail dot com> - 1.17-2 - Reduce optimization level on s390x to work around FTBFS - Install metainfo - Add -mathic patch to silence GCC warnings - Add -lto patch to silence LTO warnings
2021-01-25 Fedora Release Engineering <releng at fedoraproject dot org> - 1.17-2 - Rebuilt for https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Fedora_34_Mass_Rebuild
2021-01-16 Jerry James <loganjerry at gmail dot com> - 1.17-1 - Version 1.17 - Drop upstreamed patches: -nauty-paths, -format - Merge -gcc11 patch into mathicgb-1.0.patch
2020-10-15 Jeff Law <law at redhat dot com> - 1.16-2 - Add missing #includes for gcc-11
2020-08-31 Jerry James <loganjerry at gmail dot com> - 1.16-1 - Version 1.16 - Drop upstreamed patch: -xdg_open - Add -ulimit patch for the slower builders - Add -format and -rightarrow patches - Bundle packages due to garbage collector crashes: linbox, memtailor, mathic - Drop the XEmacs subpackage; XEmacs support no longer works
2020-08-16 Iñaki Úcar <iucar at fedoraproject dot org> - 1.15.1.0-5 - https://fedoraproject.org/wiki/Changes/FlexiBLAS_as_BLAS/LAPACK_manager
